 isaki pushti video main dikhe kai kats se hoti he
 About 1 viral on social media
 23 secont ke video main takreeban 15 se 17 cat hai, jo is baat ke sanket dete hai ki pakistani ne apane anuroop maahaul banavaane ke liye is video ko record karavaaya he or isamen kaat-chhaant kii he
 After watching this video, it will be clear why Pakistan has finally recorded this video
 kul milakar abhinandan ke video se ek baar phir pakistan kii pole khul ja rahi he ki usne apane manmutabik video banavaane ke liye kats kii bharmar laga di
 In this video, it is clearly visible how the video tries to break the flow of Abhinandan in an attempt to cut it
 agar aap gaur se is video ko dekhengo to paaenge ki is video main kareeb 15 se zyada cat hai, jo is baat kii tasdik karte hai ki pakistan ne video se chhedchhad kii he or abhinandan ke bayaan ko jabaran record karavaaya he
 On social media too, people are fiercely cursing Pakistan for this propaganda of Pakistan
 soshal media par logon ne kaaphi gussa jaahir kiya or pakistani pradhanmantri imran khan kii aalochana kar rahe hai
 According to information received from the sources, the delay in handing the Indian pilot Abhinandan to India was because the Pakistani authorities asked him to record the statement on camera
 yani yah video hi abhinandan kii deree kii vajah bana, jiske liye pakistan ada tha

 tippaniyan He said that if the BJP gets an absolute majority in the general election and if there is a bottleneck in the construction of the Ram temple, then the party can also amend the constitution for this

 pehali kii AIADMK ke taqariban sabhi vidhayak chaahate hai ki kisi bhi parivaar kaa party yaa sarkaar par varchasv na ho or saath hi ek samiti kaa gathan kiya ja rahaa he jo ye tay karegi ki AIADMK ke agle mahasachiv ke saath-saath duusare offis dharak koun honge
 This means that Sasikala, who is lodged in Bengaluru jail, will be removed from the party's general secretary and along with her nephew Dinakaran will also have to step down from the post of AIADMK deputy general secretary
 iske saath hi rajya ke purv mukhyamantri or AIADMK ke baagi o panniraselvam or unke samarthakon kii party main vaapasi kaa darwaja khulaa gaya he, kyonki panniraselvam shuru se kah rahe hai ki mukhyamantri ke pad kii unhen chaah nahin, bas wo shashikala parivaar ko satta or party se dur rakhana chaahate hai
 Earlier on Monday morning, Delhi Police accused Sasikala's nephew and party deputy general secretary Dinakaran of bribing a man for the party symbol and also arrested one
 iske baad tamilnadu main siyasat tej ho gai
 Both the case against Dinakaran and Sasikala being imprisoned became a burden for the party and the government, whether it was the Chief Minister or other ministers and senior officials
 
 
 unhen bade faisle se pehle na sirf dinakaran or shashikala ke pati em natarajan se salaah leni padati thi, balki kehete hai ki bengalooru bhi aana padataa tha
 
 isse bhi mantriyon main khaasaa rosh tha

 Lok Sabha Speaker Sumitra Mahajan has arranged that 'godse' is no longer a unparliamentary word except for mention of 'nathuram Godse'
 sansad ne 1956 main is shabd ke istemaal par pratibandh laga diya tha
 Mahatma Gandhi was assassinated by Nathuram Godse in 1948 in New Delhi
 pratibandh hataane kaa aadesh guuruuvaar ko paarit hua
 This has brought great relief to Shiv Sena MP from Nashik Hemant Tukaram Godse, who demanded the removal of the word 'godse' from the list of 'non-parliamentary words'
 hemanth tukaraam godse ne donon sadanon ke peethasin adhikariyon ko likhe patron main is baat par aashcharya jataayaa tha ki kisi saansad ke upnaam ko 'asansadeey' kaise mana ja saktaa he
 He insisted on removing the word from the list of unparliamentary words, saying, "it is definitely not my fault that my surname is Godse and apart from that i cannot change and change it as it is my paternal surname
" ' He argued that the ban 'places an undue stigma on my surname and my ancestors
 ' unhone kaha ki godse samudaay ke badi sankhya main log hai jo maharashtra ke vibhinn hisson main rahete hai or vah bhi isi samudaay ke hai
 The comments shivasena saansad ne khud ko tab ajeeb sthiti main paaya jab rajyasabha ke up sabhapati ne sheetakaaleen satr ke dauraan ek sadsy ko 'godse' shabd istemaal karne se roak diya tha, kyonki vah asansadeey tha
 The member came to know that Parliament had decided in 1956 to ban the word 'godse'
 iske baad loksabhaa adhyaksh ne yah aadesh paarit kiya he, 'ab naam 'godse' ko upnaam ke rup main asansadeey nahin kaha jayega
 Mentioning only 'nathuram Godse' would be unparliamentary
 iske anuroop hi suchi main parivartan kiya jayega

 to vahiin hatya kaa kaaran kaaphi zyada chaunkaa dene vaala nikal kar saamne aayaa he
 Actually, the body of lawyer Ajay Mudgal, living in Modinagar area of ghaziabad, was found in Baghpat two days ago
 bataaya ja rahaa tha ki unki hatya gaadi main kii gai he
 However, it was initially revealed that Ajay Mudgal was killed in a taxi
 lekin police ne aaj maamle kaa aupchaarik khulaasa kiya or kaha ki is maamle main deepak naam ke driver ko giraftaar kiya gaya he
 Deepak is the same driver whom Ajay Mudgal used to trust a lot and used to drive his car with him
 ghatana ke roj ajay mudgal gajiabad main ek shaadi main aae hue the
 During this, he called the driver Deepak with his car to go back to Modinagar
 or usee gaadi main baithkar vah waapas chal die
 On the way, they came to know that the driver had drunk too much
 is baat par unhone driver ko daantnaa shuru kiya to driver ne unako ulta jawaab dena shuru kar diya
 Deepak said that about this, Ajay Mudgal started abusing the driver
 driver ne kaha ki main tumhaara naukar hum, lekin gaali sahan nahin karuunga
 But Ajay Mudgal kept abusing him
 bas isi baat par gussa hue deepak ne ajay mudgal ko belt se peetna shuru kar diya
 And strangled him with the belt
 iske baad laash ko peripheral express-ve ke paas phenk diya gaya
 However, the family had suspected more than one person involved in the murder
 vahiin jab police ne aaropee ko hiraasat main liya to usne police ko bataaya ki ajay mudgal ek taxi main savaar hokar gaye the
 Therefore, the police had gone astray in its investigation
 lekin aaropee se kadi poochtacha karne ke baad puure maamle kaa khulaasa ho paaya he
 The Indian Railways has started using drones to monitor the progress of railway projects across the country from Delhi
 drone camere ke jariye sultanpur lambhua ke bich bichaai ja rahi nai railway line par najar rakhi ja rahi he
 Pictures are being taken with high resolution video cameras mounted on the drone
 khaas baat ye he ki ye video footage phone ke camaron se shoot kii ja rahi he
 Railways are going to start using drone cameras on a large scale to know the progress of all their projects across the country
 railway board ke member ejineering ve ke gupta ke mutabik drone camaron kii vajah se nae project par najar rakh paanaa aasaan ho gaya he
 With this, railway officials sitting in Delhi are able to know the progress of every day
 sultanpur lambhua kii nai railway line par rakhi ja rahi najararelway abhi sultanpur lambhua kii nai railway line or redwood or navi mumbai ke uran ke bich daali ja rahi nai railway line ke kaam par drone camaron se najar rakhe hue he
 By watching the video footage made from the drone camera, the officials sitting in Rail Bhavan are able to get a real idea of the actual work situation
 drone camaron se mili rigelt se utsahit adhikari ab desh bhar ke duusare projecton or railway brijon par najar rakhane ke liye or zyada drone camere lagane par vichaar kar rahe hai
